Abstract: Cross-domain EEG decoding remains challenging despite advances in Riemannian deep learning: covariance matrices from different subjects occupy systematically distinct regions of the SPD manifold, yet existing domain adaptation methods either require target-domain calibration data or learn subject-specific components that cannot generalise across domains. We propose dynamic Stiefel routing: a pool of $K$ expert projection filters on the Stiefel manifold, each specialised for a different region of the SPD manifold, with each input covariance routed to the most appropriate filter via cross-attention, adapting the subspace projection per sample. A central finding is that this approach, implemented naively, provably collapses to ensemble averaging: when routing weights are uniform, the adaptive filter reduces exactly to an equal-contribution combination of experts, indistinguishable from a single fixed filter. Three structural properties break this degeneracy: a symmetric anchor $W_{\mathrm{base}} \in \mathrm{St}(n,k)$ that removes proximity bias among experts; a frozen domain-discriminative query encoder that decouples routing from task optimisation; and a decoupled key alignment loss that trains expert keys toward stable domain attractors. Together they produce the first genuinely committed and domain-structured routing on SPD manifolds, with consistent gains across three datasets: balanced accuracy improves from $0.773\to 0.823$, $0.757\to 0.809$, and $0.801\to 0.839$, with the alignment strategy determined automatically by a single data-driven rule and no dataset-specific hyperparameter search.

In this paper, we generalize this framework to arbitrary state spaces. Building on this view, we develop a generalized neural transport learning approach for efficient estimation. Experiments validate the effectiveness and efficiency of the proposed method beyond continuous settings, extending to discrete and multimodal spaces as well as autoregressive settings. In order to overcome the curse of dimensionality in this rate, we extent this result to anisotropic and mixed smooth function classes. For mixed smooth Besov space $\mathcal{MB}^s_{q,r}([0,1]^d)$ with mixed smoothness $s>1/q-1/p$, we show that the approximation rate $\mathcal{O}((WL)^{-2s})$ holds up to logarithmic factors. Using these results, we also derive approximation bounds for the composition of anisotropic Besov functions. As an application, it is shown that deep ReLU neural networks can achieve minimax optimal rates up to logarithmic factors for a wide range of smooth function classes.

Abstract: We introduce the design-model framework: a way to derive efficient recurrent sequence maps from explicit assumptions about memory. In our linear-Gaussian instantiation, the \emph{Bayesian Layer} propagates both a mean and a covariance: the covariance tracks uncertainty over stored associations, steering writes toward uncertain directions, attenuating gains as evidence accumulates, and preserving confident memories. The same framework unifies several sub-quadratic recurrences. Linear attention, GLA, and Mamba-2/SSD are exact filters under one design model, whereas DeltaNet and related Delta-rule models arise as covariance-reset reductions under another. Method: 提出基于"任意时间有效推断"（anytime-valid inference）的替代框架，利用始终有效的统计量（如似然比或e值）进行分裂决策，而非传统的固定样本Hoeffding界。

Abstract: Bagging-based ensembles, most notably Adaptive Random Forests, are among the strongest performers for learning from data streams. A common denominator across these methods is their reliance on Hoeffding Trees as base learners, which grow decision trees incrementally by testing whether a candidate split is significantly better than its alternatives using concentration inequalities. Despite their empirical success, existing variants lack valid statistical guarantees. Current analyses rely on fixed-sample concentration bounds, while split decisions are made using data-dependent stopping rules, which invalidates their guarantees and can drive the probabilty of incorrect splits to one. We introduce a principled alternative based on anytime-valid inference. Our method provides: (i) anytime-valid control of false splits under arbitrary data streams, including non-stationary settings; (ii) finite commitment time under a predictive advantage; and (iii) under stationary i.i.d. data, risk is monotone decreasing and strictly improves at every split. Method: 提出Entropic Projection Alignment (EPA)，通过匹配源域和目标域之间精心选择的矩（moment matching），同时最小化源分布的KL散度。该优化问题具有唯一闭式解的重要性权重，并通过隐式方差控制实现鲁棒性。

Result: 大量实验表明EPA在性能估计、特征归因和域适应三个任务上均持续优于现有基线方法，同时具备显著的计算效率优势，并提供了强有力的理论保证。

Conclusion: 矩匹配足以实现对分布偏移的可靠估计和适应，无需恢复完整的密度比；EPA提供了一个统一、高效且理论完备的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose a unified framework for addressing three key challenges of distribution shift: (1) estimating a model's performance on an unlabeled target domain, (2) explaining the shift by identifying the features responsible, and (3) improving the target domain performance. Our method, Entropic Projection Alignment (EPA), aligns the source distribution to the target by matching carefully selected moments while simultaneously minimising the KL divergence from the source. This formulation yields a unique closed-form solution for importance weights, achieving robustness through implicit variance control. Drawing on domain adaptation theory, we establish that moment matching is sufficient for reliable estimation and adaptation, avoiding the need for full density ratio recovery. Extensive experiments, together with strong theoretical guarantees, demonstrate that EPA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines while offering substantial computational efficiency.

Motivation: 成分数据必须通过对数比分析，但中心化对数比变换中几何均值的引入导致单个成分污染会扩散到所有坐标。现有欧几里得空间中的单元鲁棒方法不能直接适用于成分数据，需要建立单形空间特有的污染理论。

Method: 基于乘法扰动的尺度不变污染模型，结合传播定理证明原始成分污染导致对数比向量产生秩1偏移。通过理论分析比较单形与欧几里得空间的单元崩溃值，推导出变差矩阵的单元影响函数。

Result: (1) 单污染成分导致对数比向量秩1偏移，方向由对比矩阵决定；(2) 标准欧几里得单元鲁棒方法在单形污染机制下不适定；(3) 单形上单元崩溃值降低(D-1)/D倍；(4) 变差矩阵的单元影响函数中，污染单个成分会膨胀对应行和列。

Conclusion: 该理论为单形空间上的单元鲁棒方法奠定了数学基础，并指出变差矩阵的影响函数可作为诊断工具识别受污染成分。

Abstract: Compositional data must be analysed through log-ratios: scale invariance, the defining axiom of the field, leaves no alternative. The centred log-ratio divides by the geometric mean of every part, so a single contaminated component shifts every centred-log-ratio coordinate at once, displacing the log-ratio vector by a fixed amount that no choice of coordinates can reduce. We develop a theory of cellwise contamination on the simplex around this observation. A scale-invariant contamination model built from multiplicative perturbation combines with a propagation theorem showing that corruption of a single raw part induces a rank-one shift of the log-ratio vector, with direction determined by the contrast matrix. The resulting perturbation pattern is not equivalent to any independent cellwise contamination model in log-ratio coordinates -- so standard Euclidean cellwise methods applied to log-ratios are ill-posed under the simplex contamination mechanism. For estimators whose Euclidean cellwise breakdown is witnessed by a column-concentrated configuration -- a class including MCD, $S$-, $τ$-, and coordinate-wise $M$-estimators of location and scatter -- the cellwise breakdown value on the simplex is reduced by the factor $(D-1)/D$ relative to its Euclidean counterpart, a reduction that is tight and arises purely from the normalisation mismatch between $nD$ raw cells and $n(D-1)$ ilr cells. The cellwise influence function for the variation matrix carries a diagnostic fingerprint: contamination of a single part inflates exactly one row and column, identifying the responsible component. These results form the theoretical foundation for cellwise-robust methods on the simplex; a companion paper develops a cellwise-robust PCA estimator that exploits the propagation geometry and demonstrates it on simulated and geochemical data.

</details>

# econ.EM [[Back]](#toc)

### [376] [The Markup falsification Adaptative Set](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30493)
*Santiago Acerenza,Nestor Gandelman*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在标准假设被证伪时，仍能通过连续松弛假设条件来恢复企业加成率（markup）识别集的方法，无需额外假设即可推广经典估计量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典De Loecker & Warzynski (2012)加成率估计程序在实际应用中常因假设不成立而被证伪，但缺乏系统性的修正方法。

Method: 对标准假设进行连续松弛（continuous relaxations），计算松弛参数下非证伪模型的加成率值，从而得到加成率的识别集。

Result: 获得了加成率的识别集，该集合将经典基线估计量推广到假设可能被证伪的情形。

Conclusion: 该方法为研究者提供了一种建设性的修正途径，无需施加额外假设即可应对模型误设问题，并用智利数据进行了实证验证。

Abstract: In this paper we provide a constructive way for researchers to salvage the classic De Loecker and Warzynski (2012) markup recovery procedure when falsified. To do this, we consider continuous relaxations of the standard assumptions behind markup estimation. By computing the values of the markup as a function of the relaxations across the set of non-falsified models, we obtain an identified set for the markup which generalizes the standard baseline markup estimand to account for possible falsification without the need to impose additional assumptions. We illustrate our results using Chilean data from Raval (2023).

</details>


### [377] [Rectified Linear Unit Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30609)
*Tatsushi Oka*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文提出ReLU回归框架，通过投影ReLU变换后的结果变量到协变量上，直接估计条件结果分布的积分泛函，并利用其凸共轭恢复积分条件分位数函数，从而实现对任意概率水平子区间上平均分位数处理效应的识别与推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对条件分布积分泛函的估计通常依赖强分布假设或无法处理非连续结果变量，且对平均分位数处理效应等分布参数的识别与推断存在局限，需要更一般化的框架。

Method: 提出ReLU回归方法，将ReLU变换后的结果变量对协变量进行投影，得到闭式估计量；通过Legendre-Fenchel变换得到凸共轭，恢复积分条件分位数函数；利用Hadamard方向可微映射的Delta方法进行推断。

Result: 建立了估计量的一致渐近分布理论，实现了对共轭泛函的推断，并拓展到平均分位数处理效应的识别与推断，适用于任意概率水平子区间。

Conclusion: 该方法仅需温和的分布假设，可处理非连续结果，拓宽了实证研究中可用的分布参数集合。

Abstract: This paper develops a regression framework for the direct estimation of integrated functionals of conditional outcome distributions. The proposed method, termed rectified linear unit (ReLU) regression, projects the ReLU-transformed outcome onto covariates and admits a closed-form estimator. Its population regression function coincides with the integrated conditional distribution function of the outcome, and its convex conjugate, obtained via the Legendre-Fenchel transformation, recovers the integrated conditional quantile function. Both the regression and its conjugate require only mild distributional assumptions and accommodate non-continuous outcomes. We establish the uniform asymptotic distribution of the estimator and develop inference for the conjugate functional via the delta method for Hadamard directionally differentiable maps. Building on these results, we establish identification and inference for average quantile treatment effects over arbitrary subintervals of probability levels. This broadens the set of distributional parameters available to empirical work.

</details>


### [378] [Moment-Based Inference for Regression with Latent Dirichlet Covariates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30718)
*Ziyu Jiang*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在LDA主题模型下游做回归时，绕过估计文档主题份额、直接估计回归系数β的方法。通过修正响应加权的词矩，并利用可交换性条件识别未知浓度参数α₀，实现了一阶段估计与有效推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统两阶段方法（先用主题模型降维，再用估计的主题份额做回归）存在两个问题：（1）主题估计的不确定性难以传播到第二阶段推断；（2）固定文档长度下，即使知道主题矩阵，也无法一致地恢复单篇文档的主题混合。这导致插值法推断不可靠。

Method: 在有限LDA模型下，若响应残差与低阶词矩正交，则响应加权词矩可做类似修正，得到监督算子直接识别回归系数β。关键难点是修正依赖未知总浓度α₀。作者证明，当k≥3个主题且满足有限探针条件时，通过"可交换性"（即真实值处修正后的词矩算子族可交换，非真实值处不可交换）可识别α₀，进而得到β的可行估计，且不确定性自然传播到β的推断中。

Result: 估计量在文档数增长、文档长度固定时具有渐进线性性质，可使用文档层面矩贡献的三明治标准误。模拟显示，在插值法主题份额回归覆盖不足时，新方法接近名义覆盖水平。应用于经济学顶级期刊数据，展示了潜在主题效应的对比推断。

Conclusion: 该工作为LDA下游回归提供了一种不依赖主题份额估计的一阶段推断框架，解决了不确定性传播和固定长度不一致性问题，且在理论和实证上均表现优于传统两阶段方法。

Abstract: Topic models are often used as dimension-reduction tools before regression, with estimated document-level topic shares treated as observed covariates. This plug-in workflow creates two inferential difficulties: valid inference requires a regular first-stage-to-second-stage expansion that propagates topic-estimation uncertainty, and, at fixed document length, a document's topic mixture cannot be consistently recovered from its own words even when the population topic matrix is known. Corrected spectral moment methods for latent Dirichlet allocation (LDA) offer a starting point: when the total Dirichlet concentration is known, low-order word moments can be corrected to yield operators diagonal in the latent topic basis. We extend this to downstream regression. Under a finite LDA model with response residuals orthogonal to the low-order token moments used for identification, response-weighted word moments admit the same correction, and the resulting supervised operator identifies the regression coefficient $β$ directly, without estimating document-level topic shares. The main obstacle is that the correction depends on the unknown total concentration $α_0$. We show that, for $k\ge3$ topics and under a generic finite-probe condition, $α_0$ is identified by commutativity: at the true value a family of corrected word-moment operators commute, whereas away from it they generically do not. This yields a feasible estimator and lets uncertainty in $\hatα_0$ propagate into inference for $β$. The estimator is asymptotically linear as the number of documents grows with fixed document length, with sandwich standard errors from document-level moment contributions. Simulations show near-nominal coverage where plug-in topic-share regressions can undercover, and an application to top economics journals illustrates contrast inference for latent topic effects.

</details>
